### Simultaneous Substitution

### Reflexive and transitive closure

### Lookup 

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9551" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Problem3._∋_⦂_"></a><a id="9556" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9556" class="Datatype Operator">_∋_⦂_</a> <a id="9562" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8872" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="9572" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8803" class="Function">Id</a> <a id="9577" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8693" class="Datatype">Type</a> <a id="9584" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9586" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="9590" class="Keyword">where</a>

    <a id="Problem3._∋_⦂_.Z"></a><a id="9601" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9601" class="InductiveConstructor">Z</a> <a id="9603" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9605" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9607" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9608" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9608" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9610" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9612" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9613" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="9623" class="Comment">--------------------</a>
      <a id="9650" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9608" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9654" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8916" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9610" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9658" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#8916" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⦂</a> <a id="9660" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9612" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9556" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="9664" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9610" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9556" class="Datatype Operator">⦂</a> <a id="9668" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/Exam.md %}{% raw %}#9612" class="Bound">A</a>
